e
 the feature by which an app takes some permission from you before it is installed in your smartphone so that it can monitor your smartphone and your activities

 inkaa muqabla neshnal conference ke hasanan masudi se he

 raajnneetik prishthbhumi1967 main vajood main ai anantnag seat se congress ke varisht netaaon main shumaar mohammad shafi kuraishi jite the
 He was a Member of Parliament for three consecutive terms (1967, 71 and 77)
 iske baad yah seat jammu kashmir neshnal conference ke hisse main chali gai
 In 1980, Ghulam Rasool Kochak of the National Conference, Begum Akbar Jahan Abdullah of the National Conference in 1984 and PL Handu of the National Conference in 1989 became mps
 1996 main hue chunaav main is seat se janata dal ke tikat par mohammad makabool saansad chune gaye
 After this, in 1998, Mufti Mohammad Sayeed managed to win on a Congress ticket
 1999 main yah seat phir neshnal conference ke paas aa gai or ali mohammad nike saansad bane
 In 2004, Mehbooba Mufti of the Peoples Democratic Party won this seat
 2009 main is seat se neshnal conference ke mirza mehboob beg jite
 Mehbooba Mufti was re-elected from this seat in the 2014 general election on a PDP ticket
 saamaajik tanabannantnag loksabhaa seat main 16 vidhansabha kshetra (traal, shopiyaan, devsar, pampor, nurabad, doru, pahalgam, vaachi, pulavama, kulgaam, kokarnag, bijabehaara, rajapora, homashalibug, shangus, anantnag) aate hai
 During the 2014 assembly elections, of these, PDP has 11 seats (tral, Shopian, Pampore, Noorabad, Doru, Kokernag, Bijbehara, Rajpora, Anantnag, Wachi, Kokernag), National Conference two seats (pahalgam, Homashulabug), Congress also two seats ( Devsar, Shangus) and CPE managed to win one seat (kulgam)
 is seat par matadaataaon kii sankhya kareeb 13 lakh he, jinamein kareeb 6
 85 lakh men and 6
 15 lakh mahila matadaata shaamil hai
 The Congress is not contesting this seat due to its alliance with the National Conference for the last three elections
 is seat par neshnal conference or pidipi ke bich kadi takkar hoti he
 The special thing is that during the last three elections, the BJP candidate is not able to save his bail on this seat
 2014 kaa janadesh2014 ke aam chunaav main is seat se purv mukhyamantri mahabuuba mufti duusari baar saansad chuni gai thim
 He defeated Mirza Mehboob Baig of the National Conference by about 65 thousand votes
 mahabuuba ko kareeb 2 lakh vot mili the, jabaki mirza mehboob ko 1
 35 lakh votes were received
 is seat par tisare number par nirdaleey pratyaashee tanwir hossain khan 7340 vot paakar rahe the

 unhen 4720 vot mili the

 unhone pidipi ke pir mohammad hossain ko maamuli antar se haraaya tha

 2014 ke chunaav main yahaan 28 fisadi matdaan hua tha

 is chunaav se pehle traal or avantipora main kai raajnneetik hatyaein bhi hui thi

 sanyukt raashtra kii intergovernormetal panel on climet change (ipisisi) sanstha shuukravaar ko sweden main jalwaayu par maanav gatividhi ke prabhaav or bhavishya main jalwaayu parivartan ke tathy ke akalan kii report pesh karegi
 The IPCC assessment introduces the scientific basis to the government at every stage of the development of climate-related policies, which are compromised at the United Nations Climate Convention
 vishvabhar ke deshon kii sarkaron ke pratinidhi or vaigyanik stokhome main jalwaayu parivartan ke saakshyon evam iske kaaran ke akalan report ko antim rup dene ke liye baithak kar rahe hai
 The report is based on the last four assessment reports submitted by the IPCC, released after the establishment of the IPCC in 1988
 haalia report ke pehle hisse main jalwaayu parivartan ke bhautik vigyaan ke mul siddhant par baat kii gai he
 In the next one year, the IPCC will release two other portions based on thousands of best studies
 'ipisisi varking group 1' ke upaadhyaksh kindaahe ne kaha, "maanav vikaas aadhaarit jalwaayu parivartan ke vaigyanik sakshya saal dar saal majboot hue hai, jisane jalwaayu vigyaan ke kuch kshetra main anischitata or gyaan sambandhi antar rahane ke baavjood niskriyata ke gambhir parinaam par kuch anischitataayen pesh kii hai
 "comments yah report 2015 tak jalwaayu parivartan kii kisi sandhi par pahunchane or 2020 tak ise kriyanvit karne vaale deshon ke aadhaar kaa kaam karegaa
 This fifth assessment report contains the views of 831 authors and editors
 ipisisi ke akalan main sarkaar ko jalwaayu sambandhit nitiyon ke vikaas ke har str par vaigyanik aadhaar pesh kiye jate hai, jo sanyukt raashtra ke jalwaayu sammelan main samjhauta karte hai

 yah report ipisisi dwaara pesh kiye gaye pichley chaar akalan report par aadhaarit he, jo 1988 main ipisisi kii sthapana ke baad jari kiya gaya he

 agle ek saal main ipisisi do anya hisse ko jari karegi jo hajaaron shreshth adhyayanon par aadhaarit he

 vah teen baar (1967, 71 or 77) lagaataar saansad rahe

 The Social Tanabana Anantnag Lok Sabha seat consists of 16 assembly constituencies (tral, Shopian, Devsar, Pampore, Noorabad, Doru, Pahalgam, Wachi, Pulwama, Kulgam, Kokernag, Bijbehara, Rajpora, Homashulabug, Shangus, Anantnag)
